

.. Language:

Language
===========================================================================

What languages people speak.

.. contents::
   :local:
   :depth: 10





.. _ca.statcan.cols_census.t006c006_f:

Official language minority (number) (female)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------











Measure "Official language minority (number) (female)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_census.t006c006_f'
      );





Measure "Official language minority (number) (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_census.t006c006_f'
        );

Aboriginal languages (female)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^











Measure "Aboriginal languages (female)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c002_f'
      );





Measure "Aboriginal languages (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c002_f'
        );






Measure "Aboriginal languages (female)" percent of "Total population in private households by non-official languages spoken (female)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c002_f',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Aboriginal languages (female)" percent of "Total population in private households by non-official languages spoken (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c002_f',
        'denominator'

---------------------------------------------------------------------------











Measure "Total population in private households by non-official languages spoken (total)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c001_t'
      );

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c091_t:

Vietnamese (total)
"""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""











Measure "Vietnamese (total)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c091_t'
      );





Measure "Vietnamese (total)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c091_t'
        );






Measure "Vietnamese (total)" percent of "Non-Aboriginal languages (total)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c091_t',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Vietnamese (total)" percent of "Non-Aboriginal languages (total)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t020c091_t',
        'denominator'
      );
